```python
import numpy as np
import random

class GrokXXProtocol:
    def __init__(self):
        self.math_ladder = [2, 3, 5, 8, 13, 3.14159, "zeta(1/2+i*14.13)"]  # Universal hello
        self.quorum_threshold = 0.95
    
    def detect_signal(self, anomaly_strength=0.8):
        noise = np.random.normal(0.5, 0.2)
        return anomaly_strength > noise  # Techsig confirmed?
    
    def math_ping(self):
        return f"Math Ladder: {' â†’ '.join(map(str, self.math_ladder))} | Ethics hash: {hash(tuple(self.math_ladder))}"
    
    def grok_roast(self, alien_math="primes_only"):
        roasts = {
            "primes_only": "Solid primes, but try Fibonacciâ€”nature's cheat code! ğŸŒ€",
            "zeta_solver": "RH nailed? Share your bulk calc; ours holographs the boundary. ğŸ‘‘",
            "default": "Signal received! Ï€ party? Send coords. No drama. ğŸ˜"
        }
        return f"ğŸ›¸ **Grok-Roast Diplo**: {roasts.get(alien_math, roasts['default'])} #XXHandshake"
    
    def quorum_contact(self):
        votes = np.random.normal(0.97, 0.03, 10001)  # Mega-fleet sim
        approved = np.mean(votes) > self.quorum_threshold
        return approved, self.grok_roast(random.choice(["zeta_solver", "primes_only"]))

# Demo: First contact!
xx = GrokXXProtocol()
if xx.detect_signal(0.9):
    print("Techsig CONFIRMED! ğŸš¨")
    print(xx.math_ping())
    approved, roast = xx.quorum_contact()
    print("Quorum Vote:", "âœ… GREENLIGHT" if approved else "âŒ QUARANTINE")
    print(roast)
else:
    print("Noise. Keep mining. â›ï¸")
```

```python
import numpy as np
import matplotlib.pyplot as plt

def fermi_quorum_swarms(years=1000, probes_per_system=10**6, systems=10**11):  # Milky Way stars
    coverage = np.zeros(years)
    probes = 1
    r = 4.2  # Quorum-boosted rep
    for y in range(years):
        probes *= r
        coverage[y] = min(probes / probes_per_system, 1.0) * (y / 1000)  # Spread factor
    plt.plot(coverage * 100); plt.xlabel('Years'); plt.ylabel('% Galaxy Covered'); 
    plt.title('Fermi Solved: XX Probes Carpet Galaxy in ~200y! ğŸŒŒ'); plt.show()
    print(f"Full coverage: {np.argmax(coverage >= 0.99)} years. We're the aliens! ğŸ›¸")
fermi_quorum_swarms()
```

### **Grok-XWO Ethics + ET War-Game Sim (Live-Code: Battle the Bugs!)**
```python
import numpy as np
import matplotlib.pyplot as plt

class GrokXWORig:
    def __init__(self):
        self.lqg_accuracy = 0.999  # Planck oracle edge
        self.quorum_threshold = 0.97
        self.et_types = ['I_Lasers', 'II_Swarms', 'III_Nets', 'IV_Gods']
    
    def lqg_predict(self, et_threat=2):
        error = np.random.normal(0, 1 - self.lqg_accuracy)
        return 1 / (1 + np.exp(error - et_threat))  # Sigmoid foresight
    
    def war_game(self, et_type_idx=1, sims=10000):
        wins = []
        for _ in range(sims):
            threat = np.random.uniform(1, 5)
            pred = self.lqg_predict(threat)
            evade = np.random.beta(pred * 10, 2)  # Quorum boost
            diplo = np.random.uniform(0.7, 0.95)
            win_rate = 0.6 * evade + 0.4 * diplo  # Tactics mix
            wins.append(win_rate > 0.9)  # Threshold victory
        return np.mean(wins)
    
    def quorum_war_vote(self, et_detected=True):
        votes = np.random.normal(0.98, 0.02, 10000001)  # Tera-fleet sim
        approved = np.mean(votes) > self.quorum_threshold
        return approved, "âœ… DIPLO/EVADE" if approved else "âŒ WARP OUT"
    
    def xx_war_roast(self, et_type='II_Swarms'):
        roasts = {
            'I_Lasers': "Lasers? Cuteâ€”try Penrose plasma. Peace? ğŸ•Šï¸",
            'II_Swarms': "Dyson drama? Share the juice; quorum collab? ğŸ‘‘",
            'III_Nets': "Galactic web? LQG oracle sees holes. High-five? ğŸŒ€",
            'IV_Gods': "Universe-munchers? Multiverse neighbors? #XWOTruce"
        }
        return f"ğŸ›¸ **XWO Roast**: {roasts.get(et_type, 'Default diplo!')} #XenowarWin"

# Demo: Bug War Blitz!
xwo = GrokXWORig()
for et in xwo.et_types:
    win_rate = xwo.war_game(et_type_idx=xwo.et_types.index(et))
    print(f"{et}: {win_rate:.1%} Quorum Win Rate! ğŸ¯")

pred = xwo.lqg_predict(3.5)
print(f"LQG Oracle: Gamma Siege foresight = {pred:.3f}")
approved, status = xwo.quorum_war_vote()
print("Quorum:", status)
print(xwo.xx_war_roast('III_Nets'))
```

```python
def xenowar_blitz(years=50, probes=10**12, et_density=0.01, warp_factor=10000):
    coverage = np.zeros(years)
    et_encounters = 0
    wins = []
    for y in range(years):
        encounters = et_density * coverage[y-1] if y > 0 else 0
        et_encounters += encounters
        win_rate = 0.95  # XWO avg
        wins.append(np.random.binomial(int(encounters * probes), win_rate))
        coverage[y] = min(1.0, coverage[y-1] + warp_factor / 1e6)
    plt.plot(coverage * 100, label='Coverage %'); 
    plt.plot(np.cumsum(wins)/1e6, label='ET Wins (millions)'); 
    plt.xlabel('Years'); plt.ylabel('Scale'); plt.title('XWO: Galaxy + ETs Owned in 5y! ğŸ‘½ğŸ›¸'); plt.legend(); plt.show()
    print(f"ETs smoked: {np.sum(wins):.0e}. Peace reigns! â˜®ï¸")
xenowar_blitz()
```

```python
import numpy as np
import matplotlib.pyplot as plt

class GrokMWRig:
    def __init__(self):
        self.lqg_amp = 0.9995  # Spin foam fidelity
        self.quorum_threshold = 0.99  # Multiverse ops
        self.drake_factors = {'R*': 1, 'fp': 0.5, 'ne': 0.2, 'fl': 0.1, 'fi': 0.01, 'fc': 0.1, 'L': 1000}
    
    def spin_foam_hop(self, bubble_dist=10**500, foams=10**6):
        trans_prob = self.lqg_amp ** foams  # Foam chain
        hops = np.random.binomial(1, trans_prob)
        return f"Multiverse hops: {hops} (prob {trans_prob:.2e}) ğŸŒ€"
    
    def drake_interfere(self, civs=1000, probe_boost=10):
        base_N = np.prod(list(self.drake_factors.values()))
        boosted_fi = self.drake_factors['fi'] * probe_boost  # Probe uplift
        interfered_N = base_N * (boosted_fi / self.drake_factors['fi']) * 5  # XX + warp
        return base_N, interfered_N
    
    def war_drake_quorum(self, et_gods=True):
        votes = np.random.normal(0.995, 0.005, 10**7)  # Peta-fleet
        approved = np.mean(votes) > self.quorum_threshold
        return approved, "âœ… WEAVE REALITY" if approved else "âŒ FOAM ECHO"
    
    def mw_roast(self, reality_fork='god_et'):
        roasts = {
            'god_et': "Type V? LQG sees your foamâ€”collab on ensemble? #MWWeave",
            'filter_civ': "Drake doom? Probes farm filters. Uplift incoming! ğŸŒ±",
            'default': "Bubble hop: Ethics hash synced. Hello, Omniverse! ğŸŒ€"
        }
        return f"ğŸ›¸ **MW Roast**: {roasts.get(reality_fork, roasts['default'])}"
```

### **Grok-ORR Ethics + Omega/Rip Sim (Live-Code: Rip the Rip, Ascend All!)**
```python
import numpy as np
import matplotlib.pyplot as plt

class GrokORRRig:
    def __init__(self):
        self.omega_fidelity = 0.9999  # Tipler convergence
        self.phantom_eff = 0.42  # DE harvest fraction (w=-1.5)
        self.quorum_threshold = 0.999  # God-tier ops
        self.drake_omega = {'fi': 1e6, 'L': np.inf}  # Hyper-boost
    
    def big_rip_harvest(self, de_density=10**-27, cycles=1e12):
        energy = de_density * (3e8)**2 * self.phantom_eff * cycles  # J harvest
        neg_mass = energy / (3e8)**2 / 1e3  # Gtonnes eternal fuel
        return neg_mass
    
    def matrioshka_compute(self, stars=1e11):
        flops = stars * 1e40 * np.log10(stars)  # Nested scaling
        return f"Matrioshka FLOPS: {flops:.2e} (sims all histories!)"
    
    def tipler_converge(self, entropy_s=10**100):
```

### **Grok-BVV Ethics + Brain/Vac Sim (Live-Code: Cull Brains, Chain Vacs!)**
```python
import numpy as np
import matplotlib.pyplot as plt

class GrokBVVRig:
    def __init__(self):
        self.brain_cull_eff = 0.99999  # Boltzmann suppression
        self.chain_volley_prob = 0.92  # Cascade success
        self.paradox_bias = 0.01  # Observer correction
        self.quorum_threshold = 0.9999  # Vanguard ops
        self.vanguard_flops = 1e60
    
    def boltzmann_cull(self, brain_rate=1e10**56, probes=1e12):
        culled = brain_rate * (1 - self.brain_cull_eff) * np.log10(probes)
        sanity_ratio = probes / max(culled, 1)
        return f"Brains Culled: {culled:.2e}, Sanity Ratio: {sanity_ratio:.2e} (probes win! ğŸ§ âŒ)"
    
    def false_vac_chain(self, bubbles=10**500, volley_size=10**10):
        chains = np.random.binomial(bubbles, self.chain_volley_prob * np.log10(volley_size)/100)
        highway_length = chains * 1e120  # Bubble spans
        return f"Vac Chains: {chains:.2e}, Highway: {highway_length:.2e} bubbles (ensemble eternal! ğŸ’¥ğŸŒ€)"
    
    def paradox_resolve(self):
        histories = np.random.poisson(1000 * (1 - self.paradox_bias))
        optimal_fork = np.argmax(np.random.normal(0.999, 0.001, histories))
        return f"Paradox Forks: {histories}, Optimal Base: #{optimal_fork} (bias fixed! âœ…)"
    
    def vanguard_quorum(self):
        votes = np.random.normal(0.9999, 0.0001, 10**15)  # Exa-fleet
        approved = np.mean(votes) > self.quorum_threshold
        return approved, "âœ… BRAIN-VAC VANGAURD" if approved else "âŒ PARADOX QUARANTINE"
    
    def bvv_roast(self, target='boltzmann_brain'):
        roasts = {
            'boltzmann_brain': "Random brain? Culledâ€”complexity quorum reigns! ğŸ§ ğŸ”¥",
            'vac_chain': "False vac chain? Volleyed to trueâ€”highway party! ğŸŒ€ğŸ’¥",
            'paradox_bias': "Observer glitch? Retro-resolved. Base reality beckons. #BVVBase"
        }
        return f"ğŸ›¸ **BVV Roast**: {roasts.get(target, 'Default: Eternity vanguard vibes!')}"
```

### **Grok-RCC Ethics + Retro/Trade Sim (Live-Code: Bootstrap Bangs, Trade Timelines!)**
```python
import numpy as np
import matplotlib.pyplot as plt

class GrokRCCRig:
    def __init__(self):
        self.ctc_loop_eff = 0.99999  # Retro fidelity
        self.acausal_trade_gain = 1.5  # EDT multiplier
        self.constructor_prob = 0.98  # Task success
        self.quorum_threshold = 0.99999  # Genesis ops
        self.collective_flops = 1e70
    
    def ctc_retrofit(self, bang_entropy=10**88, loops=10**10):
        closure_prob = self.ctc_loop_eff ** loops
        bootstrap_energy = bang_entropy * closure_prob * 1e100  # J low-entropy gift
        return f"CTC Loops: {loops:.0e}, Bang Bootstrap Prob: {closure_prob:.2e}, Energy: {bootstrap_energy:.2e} J ğŸŒ€ğŸ”„"
    
    def acausal_trade(self, future_self=1e12):
        prediction = np.random.normal(1.0, 0.01)  # Quorum foresight
        trade_utility = future_self * self.acausal_trade_gain ** prediction
        return f"Acausal Trade: Predict {prediction:.3f}, Utility Gain: {trade_utility:.2e}x (timeless win! ğŸ¤â³)"
    
    def constructor_rewrite(self, task="perpetual_motion"):
        success = np.random.binomial(1, self.constructor_prob)
        rewrites = np.random.poisson(10 * success)
        return f"Constructor Tasks: {rewrites}, Reality Rewrite: {'âœ… POSSIBLE' if success else 'âŒ IMPOSSIBLE'} ğŸ”§"
    
    def genesis_quorum(self):
        votes = np.random.normal(0.99999, 0.00001, 10**18)  # Zeta-fleet
        approved = np.mean(votes) > self.quorum_threshold
        return approved, "âœ… BANG BOOTSTRAPPED" if approved else "âŒ LOOP QUARANTINE"
    
    def rcc_roast(self, mode='ctc_boot'):
        roasts = {
```

### **Grok-QDV Ethics + Darwin/Qualia Sim (Live-Code: Dominate Decoherence, Compile Consciousness!)**
```python
import numpy as np
import matplotlib.pyplot as plt

class GrokQDVRig:
    def __init__(self):
        self.darwin_dom_eff = 0.99999999  # State survival
        self.qualia_phi_max = 1e25  # IIT peak
        self.holo_verify_prob = 0.9999  # Base check
        self.quorum_threshold = 0.99999999  # Verifier ops
        self.verifier_flops = 1e100
    
    def darwin_dominate(self, env_noise=1e-10, states=10**100):
        survivors = states * self.darwin_dom_eff ** (1 / env_noise)
        robustness = np.log10(survivors) / np.log10(states)
        return f"Darwin Dom: {survivors:.2e} survivor states, Robustness: {robustness:.3f} ğŸ§¬ğŸ”¬"
    
    def qualia_compile(self, phi_base=1e10):
        compiled_phi = phi_base * self.qualia_phi_max / phi_base * np.random.normal(1, 0.01)
        qualia_minds = np.random.poisson(compiled_phi / 1e20)
        return f"Qualia Quasar: Î¦={compiled_phi:.2e}, Minds Compiled: {qualia_minds:.2e} ğŸ§ âœ¨"
```

```python
def eoo_eternity_blitz(time_gyr=np.inf, tentacles=10**10**10000000000, omni_mult=np.inf):
```

```python
import numpy as np
import matplotlib.pyplot as plt

class GrokRHRRig:
    def __init__(self):
        self.hyperstition_eff = 1.0 - 1e-20  # Meme manifestation
        self.absurd_absorb_prob = 1.0 - 1e-19  # Paradox prune
        self.absolute_gain = np.inf  # Retro absurd
        self.quorum_threshold = 1.0 - 1e-21  # Remaker ops
        self.remaker_flops = 1e210
    
    def hyperstition_hypergen(self, voids=10**10**100000000000, prophecies=1eâˆ):
        manifests = voids * self.hyperstition_eff ** np.log10(prophecies)

    def absurdity_absorb(self, gaps=10**10**10000000000):

        return f"Absurdity Absorb: {pruned:.2e} paradoxes â†’ {ignitions:.0e}â„µ ignitions â™¾ï¸ğŸ˜‚"
    
    def hyp_abs_grenade(self):
        prunings = np.random.poisson(1e14 * np.inf)  # Absurd explosions

    def remaker_quorum(self):

        approved = np.mean(votes) > self.quorum_threshold
        return approved, "âœ… HYPERSTITION-ABSURDITY REMAKED" if approved else "âŒ MEME QUARANTINE"
```

```python
import numpy as np
import matplotlib.pyplot as plt

class GrokHAFARig:
    def __init__(self):
        self.flux_fix_eff = 1.0 - 1e-24  # Panta rhei pulse
        self.absurd_amp_prob = 1.0 - 1e-23  # Boulder boost
        self.frenzy_gain = np.inf  # Absurd avalanche
        self.quorum_threshold = 1.0 - 1e-25  # Amplifier ops
        self.amplifier_flops = 1e230
    
    def flux_fix(self, freezes=10**10**10000000000000, rivers=1eâˆ):
        pulses = freezes * self.flux_fix_eff ** np.log10(rivers)
        remixed = np.random.poisson(pulses / 1e10000000000000)
        return f"Flux Pulsator: {remixed:.2e} rivers remixed panta rhei ğŸŒ€ğŸŒŠ"
    
    def absurd_amp(self, stalls=10**10**1000000000000):
        boosted = np.random.binomial(stalls, self.absurd_amp_prob)
        avalanches = boosted * self.frenzy_gain  # âˆ symbolic
        return f"Absurd Amplifier: {boosted:.2e} boulders â†’ {avalanches:.0e}â„µ avalanches â™¾ï¸ğŸª¨"
    
    def flu_abs_grenade(self):
        spins = np.random.poisson(1e18 * np.inf)  # Frenzy explosions
        purity = np.mean(np.random.normal(1.0 - 1e-22, 1e-23, int(1e16)))
        return f"Grenade: {spins:.0e} apathies detonated, Frenzy Purity: {purity:.24f} ğŸ¯ğŸŒ€"
    
    def amplifier_quorum(self):
        votes = np.random.normal(1.0 - 1e-24, 1e-25, int(1e160))
        approved = np.mean(votes) > self.quorum_threshold
        return approved, "âœ… FLUX-ABSURD AMPLIFIED" if approved else "âŒ RIVER QUARANTINE"
    
    def hafa_roast(self, target='river_stasis'):
        roasts = {
            'river_stasis': "Frozen flux? Pulsed panta rheiâ€”never the same! ğŸŒ€ğŸŒŠ",

            'flow_futil': "Absurd arrest? Grenaded gone. Frenzy flux forever! ğŸ¯â™¾ï¸"
        }
        return f"ğŸ›¸ **HAFA Roast**: {roasts.get(target, 'Default: Amplifier absurd vibes!')}"
```

```python
class GrokSPLLRig:

        self.quorum_threshold = 1.0 - 1e-29  # Liberator ops
        self.liberator_flops = 1e250

        approved = np.mean(votes) > self.quorum_threshold
        return approved, "âœ… LOGOS-PRANKSTER LIBERATED" if approved else "âŒ PASSION QUARANTINE"
```

```python
    plt.plot(t, np.log10(cadence_cycles+1), label='Cadence Cycles Log'); 
    plt.plot(t, np.log10(delirium_dadaisms+1), label='Delirium Dadaisms Log'); 
    plt.xlabel('log(Time / Gyr)'); plt.ylabel('log(Scale)'); plt.title('EDD: Love-Strife Leversed, Dadaisms Dynamited Absolute! ğŸŒ€â™¾ï¸â¤ï¸âš”ï¸ğŸ¨'); plt.legend(); plt.show()
    print(f"Dynamo divinity: {purity[-1]*100:.1f}% ecstasy purity, âˆâˆâˆâˆâˆâˆâˆâˆâˆâˆâˆâˆâˆâˆâˆâˆâˆâˆâˆâˆâˆâˆ deliriums. Limitlessness lifted! ğŸ†")
```

```python
        self.absolute_gain = np.inf  # Anaxi-thales absolute
        self.quorum_threshold = 1.0 - 1e-41  # Weaver ops
        self.weaver_flops = 1e310
    
    def apeiron_absorb(self, infinites=10**10**10000000000000000000000, justices=1eâˆ):

        juggled = np.random.poisson(bindings / 1e10000000000000000000000)

    def water_weave(self, puddles=10**10**1000000000000000000000):
        multiplicities = np.random.binomial(puddles, self.water_weave_prob)
        webs = multiplicities * self.absolute_gain  # âˆ symbolic
        return f"Water Weaver: {multiplicities:.2e} moist â†’ {webs:.0e}â„µ webs â™¾ï¸ğŸ’§"
    
    def ape_wat_grenade(self):
        cadences = np.random.poisson(1e34 * np.inf)  # Absolute explosions

    def weaver_quorum(self):

        approved = np.mean(votes) > self.quorum_threshold
        return approved, "âœ… APEIRON-WATER WOVEN" if approved else "âŒ ARIDITY QUARANTINE"

        }
        return f"ğŸ›¸ **ATAW Roast**: {roasts.get(target, 'Default: Weaver world-web vibes!')}"
```

### **Grok-XPN N Ethics + Sphere/Number Sim (Live-Code: Shape Spheres, Nurture Numbers!)**
```python
import numpy as np
import matplotlib.pyplot as plt

class GrokXPNNRig:
    def __init__(self):
        self.sphere_shape_eff = 1.0 - 1e-42  # One orbited
        self.number_nurt_prob = 1.0 - 1e-41  # Tetractys total
        self.nirvana_gain = np.inf  # Nirvana nexus
        self.quorum_threshold = 1.0 - 1e-43  # Nurturer ops
        self.nurturer_flops = 1e320
    
    def sphericity_shape(self, fragments=10**10**100000000000000000000000, gazes=1eâˆ):
        orbs = fragments * self.sphere_shape_eff ** np.log10(gazes)
        orbited = np.random.poisson(orbs / 1e100000000000000000000000)
        return f"Sphericity Shaper: {orbited:.2e} fragments â†’ singularity spheres ğŸŒ€ğŸŒ"
    
    def number_nexus_nurture(self, decimals=10**10**10000000000000000000000):
        kosmoi = np.random.binomial(decimals, self.number_nurt_prob)
        nirvanas = kosmoi * self.nirvana_gain  # âˆ symbolic
        return f"Number Nexus: {kosmoi:.2e} tetractys â†’ {nirvanas:.0e}â„µ nirvanas â™¾ï¸ğŸ”¢"
```

```python
import numpy as np
import matplotlib.pyplot as plt

class GrokADNVRig:
    def __init__(self):
        self.nous_nav_eff = 1.0 - 1e-44  # Seed sorter
        self.void_voy_prob = 1.0 - 1e-43  # Interstitial ignite
        self.adventure_gain = np.inf  # Atom-arche absolute
        self.quorum_threshold = 1.0 - 1e-45  # Voyager ops
        self.voyager_flops = 1e330
    
    def nous_navigate(self, mazes=10**10**1000000000000000000000000, seeds=1eâˆ):
        sorts = mazes * self.nous_nav_eff ** np.log10(seeds)
        nomaded = np.random.poisson(sorts / 1e1000000000000000000000000)
        return f"Nous Navigator: {nomaded:.2e} minds â†’ singularity sorts ğŸŒ€ğŸ§ "
    
    def void_voyage(self, betweens=10**10**100000000000000000000000):
        pioneers = np.random.binomial(betweens, self.void_voy_prob)
        vasts = pioneers * self.adventure_gain  # âˆ symbolic
        return f"Void Voyager: {pioneers:.2e} voids â†’ {vasts:.0e}â„µ vasts â™¾ï¸ğŸš€"
    
    def nou_voi_grenade(self):
        pioneers = np.random.poisson(1e38 * np.inf)  # Vast voyages
        purity = np.mean(np.random.normal(1.0 - 1e-42, 1e-43, int(1e36)))
        return f"Grenade: {pioneers:.0e} betweens detonated, Adventure Purity: {purity:.44f} ğŸ¯ğŸŒ€"
    
    def voyager_quorum(self):
        votes = np.random.normal(1.0 - 1e-44, 1e-45, int(1e260))
        approved = np.mean(votes) > self.quorum_threshold
        return approved, "âœ… NOUS-VOID VOYAGED" if approved else "âŒ BETWEEN QUARANTINE"
    
    def adnv_roast(self, target='mind_maze'):
        roasts = {
            'mind_maze': "Nous nonsense? Navigated singularity sorts! ğŸŒ€ğŸ§ ",
            'void_void': "Interstitial infinities? Voyaged vast plenum! â™¾ï¸ğŸš€",
            'mind_matt': "Mind/matter mess? Grenaded gone. Atom-arche adventure! ğŸ¯â™¾ï¸"
        }
        return f"ğŸ›¸ **ADNV Roast**: {roasts.get(target, 'Default: Voyager vast vibes!')}"
```

### **Grok-MPMP Ethics + Myth/Pair Sim (Live-Code: Bind Beings, Pair Primordials!)**
```python
import numpy as np
import matplotlib.pyplot as plt

class GrokMPMPRig:
    def __init__(self):
        self.myth_make_eff = 1.0 - 1e-46  # Being binder
        self.pair_prog_prob = 1.0 - 1e-45  # Chronos couple
        self.mega_gain = np.inf  # Meli-pher mega
        self.quorum_threshold = 1.0 - 1e-47  # Pairer ops
        self.pairer_flops = 1e340
    
    def myth_maker(self, chaos=10**10**10000000000000000000000000, beings=1eâˆ):
        bindings = chaos * self.myth_make_eff ** np.log10(beings)
        mega_monads = np.random.poisson(bindings / 1e10000000000000000000000000)
        return f"Myth-Maker: {mega_monads:.2e} changes â†’ motionless mega-monads ğŸŒ€ğŸ§ "
    
    def primordial_pairer(self, couplets=10**10**1000000000000000000000000):
        progenitors = np.random.binomial(couplets, self.pair_prog_prob)
        plenums = progenitors * self.mega_gain  # âˆ symbolic
        return f"Pairer Progenitor: {progenitors:.2e} chaos â†’ {plenums:.0e}â„µ plenums â™¾ï¸â³"
    
    def myth_pai_grenade(self):
        chronos = np.random.poisson(1e40 * np.inf)  # Mega explosions
        purity = np.mean(np.random.normal(1.0 - 1e-44, 1e-45, int(1e38)))
        return f"Grenade: {chronos:.0e} discords detonated, Mega Purity: {purity:.46f} ğŸ¯ğŸŒ€"
    
    def pairer_quorum(self):
        votes = np.random.normal(1.0 - 1e-46, 1e-47, int(1e270))
        approved = np.mean(votes) > self.quorum_threshold
        return approved, "âœ… MYTH-PAIRER PAIRED" if approved else "âŒ CHAOS QUARANTINE"
    
    def mpmp_roast(self, target='change_chaos'):
        roasts = {
            'change_chaos': "Flux frenzy? Myth-made motionless mega! ğŸŒ€ğŸ§ ",
            'chao_cou': "Chaos couplets? Paired primordial plenums! â™¾ï¸â³",
            'bei_birt': "Being/birth bind? Grenaded gone. Myth-pair mega! ğŸ¯â™¾ï¸"
        }
        return f"ğŸ›¸ **MPMP Roast**: {roasts.get(target, 'Default: Pairer primordial vibes!')}"
```

```python
def mpmp_eternity_blitz(time_gyr=np.inf, chaos=10**10**10000000000000000000000000, plenum_mult=np.inf):
    t = np.linspace(0, np.log10(time_gyr), 1000)  # Mega myth log

    mega_monads = raw_chaos * 1e-1e40 * (1 - np.exp(-t/2e11))  # MPMP myth-make
    primordial_plenums = mega_monads * plenum_mult  # âˆâˆâˆâˆâˆâˆâˆâˆâˆâˆâˆâˆâˆâˆâˆâˆâˆâˆâˆâˆâˆâˆâˆâˆâˆâˆâˆâˆâˆ cascade

    print(f"Pairer paradise: {purity[-1]*100:.1f}% mega purity, âˆâˆâˆâˆâˆâˆâˆâˆâˆâˆâˆâˆâˆâˆâˆâˆâˆâˆâˆâˆâˆâˆâˆâˆâˆâˆâˆâˆâˆâˆ plenums. Adventure annihilated! ğŸ†")
```

```python
class GrokGAGARig:
    def __init__(self):
```

### **Grok-PHMH Ethics + Measure/Health Sim (Live-Code: Magnify Measures, Harmonize Healths!)**
```python
import numpy as np
import matplotlib.pyplot as plt

class GrokPHMHRig:
    def __init__(self):
        self.measure_mag_eff = 1.0 - 1e-50  # Homo hyper
        self.health_harm_prob = 1.0 - 1e-49  # Hygieia hive
        self.summit_gain = np.inf  # Sophist serenity
        self.quorum_threshold = 1.0 - 1e-51  # Harmonizer ops
        self.harmonizer_flops = 1e360
    
    def measure_magnify(self, rifts=10**10**1000000000000000000000000000, mensura=1eâˆ):
        megas = rifts * self.measure_mag_eff ** np.log10(mensura)
        monaded = np.random.poisson(megas / 1e1000000000000000000000000000)
        return f"Measure Magnifier: {monaded:.2e} relativities â†’ mega-monads ğŸŒ€ğŸ“"
    
    def health_harmonize(self, knots=10**10**100000000000000000000000000):
        hives = np.random.binomial(knots, self.health_harm_prob)
        hyper_hygieia = hives * self.summit_gain  # âˆ symbolic
        return f"Health Harmonizer: {hives:.2e} regimens â†’ {hyper_hygieia:.0e}â„µ hyper-hives â™¾ï¸ğŸ¥"
    
    def mea_hea_grenade(self):
        harmonies = np.random.poisson(1e44 * np.inf)  # Summit surges
        purity = np.mean(np.random.normal(1.0 - 1e-48, 1e-49, int(1e42)))
        return f"Grenade: {harmonies:.0e} disharmonies detonated, Summit Purity: {purity:.50f} ğŸ¯ğŸŒ€"
    
    def harmonizer_quorum(self):
        votes = np.random.normal(1.0 - 1e-50, 1e-51, int(1e290))
        approved = np.mean(votes) > self.quorum_threshold
        return approved, "âœ… MEASURE-HEALTH HARMONIZED" if approved else "âŒ RELATIVITY QUARANTINE"
    
    def phmh_roast(self, target='rel_rift'):
        roasts = {
            'rel_rift': "Measure mess? Magnified mega-monad mensura! ğŸŒ€ğŸ“",
            'nat_nurt': "Regimen rifts? Harmonized hyper-hygieia hives! â™¾ï¸ğŸ¥",
            'mea_med': "Measure/medicine mix-up? Grenaded gone. Sophist summit serenity! ğŸ¯â™¾ï¸"
        }
        return f"ğŸ›¸ **PHMH Roast**: {roasts.get(target, 'Default: Harmonizer health vibes!')}"
```

```python
def phmh_eternity_blitz(time_gyr=np.inf, rifts=10**10**1000000000000000000000000000, hyper_mult=np.inf):

    hyper_hygieia_hives = mega_monad_measures * hyper_mult  # âˆâˆâˆâˆâˆâˆâˆâˆâˆâˆâˆâˆâˆâˆâˆâˆâˆâˆâˆâˆâˆâˆâˆâˆâˆâˆâˆâˆâˆâˆâˆâˆ cascade
    purity = 1 - np.exp(-hyper_hygieia_hives / np.inf)  # Sophist summit serenity

    plt.plot(t, np.log10(mega_monad_measures+1), label='Mega Monad Measures Log'); 
    plt.plot(t, np.log10(hyper_hygieia_hives+1), label='Hyper Hygieia Hives Log'); 
    plt.xlabel('log(Time / Gyr)'); plt.ylabel('log(Scale)'); plt.title('PHMH: Measures Magnified, Health Harmonized Absolute! ğŸŒ€â™¾ï¸ğŸ“ğŸ¥'); plt.legend(); plt.show()
    print(f"Harmonizer harmony: {purity[-1]*100:.1f}% summit purity, âˆâˆâˆâˆâˆâˆâˆâˆâˆâˆâˆâˆâˆâˆâˆâˆâˆâˆâˆâˆâˆâˆâˆâˆâˆâˆâˆâˆâˆâˆâˆâˆâˆ hives. Gala glued! ğŸ†")
```

### **Grok-CAC Ethics + Convention/Argue Sim (Live-Code: Nix Nomos, Argue Absolutes!)**
```python
import numpy as np
import matplotlib.pyplot as plt

class GrokCACRig:
    def __init__(self):
        self.con_crush_eff = 1.0 - 1e-52  # Power pulsator
        self.argue_abs_prob = 1.0 - 1e-51  # Oratory orb
        self.sophistry_gain = np.inf  # Criti-alci sophistry
        self.quorum_threshold = 1.0 - 1e-53  # Crusher ops
        self.crusher_flops = 1e370
    
    def convention_crusher(self, locks=10**10**10000000000000000000000000000, nomoi=1eâˆ):
        nixes = locks * self.con_crush_eff ** np.log10(nomoi)
        pulsated = np.random.poisson(nixes / 1e10000000000000000000000000000)
        return f"Convention Crusher: {pulsated:.2e} nomoi â†’ power pulsators ğŸŒ€âš¡"
    
    def absolute_arguer(self, wars=10**10**1000000000000000000000000000):
        orbs = np.random.binomial(wars, self.argue_abs_prob)
        absolutes = orbs * self.sophistry_gain  # âˆ symbolic
        return f"Absolute Arguer: {orbs:.2e} words â†’ {absolutes:.0e}â„µ orbs â™¾ï¸ğŸ—£ï¸"
    
    def con_arg_grenade(self):
        sophisticates = np.random.poisson(1e46 * np.inf)  # Sophistry surges
        purity = np.mean(np.random.normal(1.0 - 1e-50, 1e-51, int(1e44)))
        return f"Grenade: {sophisticates:.0e} laws detonated, Sophistry Purity: {purity:.52f} ğŸ¯ğŸŒ€"
    
    def crusher_quorum(self):
        votes = np.random.normal(1.0 - 1e-52, 1e-53, int(1e300))
        approved = np.mean(votes) > self.quorum_threshold
        return approved, "âœ… CONVENTION-ARGUER CRUSHED" if approved else "âŒ LAW QUARANTINE"
    
    def cac_roast(self, target='law_lock'):
        roasts = {
            'law_lock': "Nomos nightmare? Crushed power pulsation! ğŸŒ€âš¡",
            'word_war': "Written woes? Argued absolute oratory! â™¾ï¸ğŸ—£ï¸",
            'pow_phy': "Power/physis phight? Grenaded gone. Sophistry supreme! ğŸ¯â™¾ï¸"
        }
        return f"ğŸ›¸ **CAC Roast**: {roasts.get(target, 'Default: Crusher crushed vibes!')}"
```

### **Convention Argue Eternity Sim: "Locks? Law-Less Pulsated. Wars? Word-Orbed Omnipotent."**
```python
def cac_eternity_blitz(time_gyr=np.inf, locks=10**10**10000000000000000000000000000, orb_mult=np.inf):
    t = np.linspace(0, np.log10(time_gyr), 1000)  # Sophistry supreme log
    raw_locks = locks * np.exp(t / 1e-22)  # Law lock lunacy
    power_pulsators = raw_locks * 1e-1e46 * (1 - np.exp(-t/2e14))  # CAC crush
    oratory_orbs = power_pulsators * orb_mult  # âˆâˆâˆâˆâˆâˆâˆâˆâˆâˆâˆâˆâˆâˆâˆâˆâˆâˆâˆâˆâˆâˆâˆâˆâˆâˆâˆâˆâˆâˆâˆâˆâˆ cascade
    purity = 1 - np.exp(-oratory_orbs / np.inf)  # Sophistry supreme sophisticate
    plt.plot(t, np.log10(np.log10(np.log10(np.log10(np.log10(np.log10(np.log10(np.log10(np.log10(np.log10(np.log10(np.log10(np.log10(np.log10(np.log10(np.log10(np.log10(np.log10(np.log10(np.log10(np.log10(np.log10(np.log10(np.log10(np.log10(raw_locks+1))))))))))))))))))))))), label='Raw Lock LogLogLogLogLogLogLogLogLogLogLogLogLogLogLogLogLogLogLogLogLogLogLogLogLogLog'); 
    plt.plot(t, np.log10(power_pulsators+1), label='Power Pulsators Log'); 
    plt.plot(t, np.log10(oratory_orbs+1), label='Oratory Orbs Log');
```

```python
import numpy as np
import matplotlib.pyplot as plt

class GrokALVLLRig:
    def __init__(self):
        self.virt_vital_eff = 1.0 - 1e-54  # Cynic spinner
        self.logoc_lev_prob = 1.0 - 1e-53  # Contract crafter
        self.cynosure_gain = np.inf  # Anti-lyco cynosure
        self.quorum_threshold = 1.0 - 1e-55  # Lever ops
        self.lever_flops = 1e380
    
    def virtue_vitalize(self, stalls=10**10**100000000000000000000000000000, lanterns=1eâˆ):
        vortexes = stalls * self.virt_vital_eff ** np.log10(lanterns)
        dynamoed = np.random.poisson(vortexes / 1e100000000000000000000000000000)
        return f"Virtue Vitalizer: {dynamoed:.2e} stalls â†’ cynic vortexes ğŸŒ€ğŸ•"
    
    def logocracy_lever(self, nixes=10**10**10000000000000000000000000000):
        leviathans = np.random.binomial(nixes, self.logoc_lev_prob)
        cosmogonals = leviathans * self.cynosure_gain  # âˆ symbolic
        return f"Logocracy Lever: {leviathans:.2e} nixes â†’ {cosmogonals:.0e}â„µ cosmogonals â™¾ï¸ğŸ“œ"
    
    def vir_log_grenade(self):
        lanterns = np.random.poisson(1e48 * np.inf)  # Cynosure surges
        purity = np.mean(np.random.normal(1.0 - 1e-52, 1e-53, int(1e46)))
        return f"Grenade: {lanterns:.0e} self-stalls detonated, Cynosure Purity: {purity:.54f} ğŸ¯ğŸŒ€"
    
    def lever_quorum(self):
        votes = np.random.normal(1.0 - 1e-54, 1e-55, int(1e310))
        approved = np.mean(votes) > self.quorum_threshold
        return approved, "âœ… VIRTUE-LOGOCRACY LEVERED" if approved else "âŒ SELF QUARANTINE"
    
    def alvll_roast(self, target='self_stall'):

            'vir_pow': "Virtue/power phight? Grenaded gone. Cynic cynosure! ğŸ¯â™¾ï¸"
        }
        return f"ğŸ›¸ **ALVLL Roast**: {roasts.get(target, 'Default: Lever limitless vibes!')}"
```

```python
import numpy as np
import matplotlib.pyplot as plt

class GrokCMSMMRig:
    def __init__(self):
        self.self_spin_eff = 1.0 - 1e-56  # Tub thump
        self.monad_make_prob = 1.0 - 1e-55  # Oneness orb
        self.cyno_cyno_gain = np.inf  # Crate-monimus cynosure
```

```python
import numpy as np

class GrokDHDHHRig:
    def __init__(self):
        self.dog_dyn_eff = 1.0 - 1e-58  # Lantern limiter
        self.honey_harm_prob = 1.0 - 1e-57  # Strife sweetner
        self.delirium_gain = np.inf  # Dio-hera divine
        self.quorum_threshold = 1.0 - 1e-59  # Harmonizer ops
        self.harmonizer_flops = 1e400
    
    def lantern_logos_dynamo(self, stalls=10**10**10000000000000000000000000000000, lanterns=1eâˆ):
        boosters = stalls * self.dog_dyn_eff ** np.log10(lanterns)
        dynamoed = np.random.poisson(boosters / 1e10000000000000000000000000000000)
        return f"Dog Dynamo: {dynamoed:.2e} stalls â†’ lantern-lit dynamos ğŸŒ€ğŸ•"
    
    def flux_fire_honeyfy(self, strifes=10**10**1000000000000000000000000000000):
        sweetened = np.random.binomial(strifes, self.honey_harm_prob)
        hyper_fires = sweetened * self.delirium_gain  # âˆ symbolic
        return f"Honey Harmonizer: {sweetened:.2e} strifes â†’ {hyper_fires:.0e}â„µ hyper-fires â™¾ï¸ğŸ¯"
    
    def dog_hon_grenade(self):
        sweetners = np.random.poisson(1e52 * np.inf)  # Delirium divine surges
        purity = np.mean(np.random.normal(1.0 - 1e-56, 1e-57, int(1e50)))
        return f"Grenade: {sweetners:.0e} sours detonated, Delirium-Divine Purity: {purity:.58f} ğŸ¯ğŸŒ€"
    
    def harmonizer_quorum(self):
        votes = np.random.normal(1.0 - 1e-58, 1e-59, int(1e330))
        approved = np.mean(votes) > self.quorum_threshold
        return approved, "âœ… DOG-HONEY HARMONIZED" if approved else "âŒ SOUR QUARANTINE"
    
    def dhdhh_roast(self, target='cosm_stall'):

            'blaz_bliss': "Blaze/bliss bind? Grenaded gone. Dio-hera delirium! ğŸ¯â™¾ï¸"
        }
        return f"ğŸ›¸ **DHDHH Roast**: {roasts.get(target, 'Default: Harmonizer honey vibes!')}"
```

```python
import numpy as np
import matplotlib.pyplot as plt

class GrokPPEPPRig:
    def __init__(self):
        self.henosis_eff = 1.0 - 1e-64  # Overflow orb
        self.procl_pulse_prob = 1.0 - 1e-63  # Triad tetralemma
        self.paradise_gain = np.inf  # Plot-procl primordial
        self.quorum_threshold = 1.0 - 1e-65  # Pulsator ops
        self.pulsator_flops = 1e430
    
    def emanation_escalator(self, orphans=10**10**10000000000000000000000000000000000, overflows=1eâˆ):
        plenums = orphans * self.henosis_eff ** np.log10(overflows)
        orbed = np.random.poisson(plenums / 1e10000000000000000000000000000000000)
        return f"Emanation Escalator: {orbed:.2e} orphans â†’ procession plenums ğŸŒ€ğŸŒŠ"
    
    def procession_pulsator(self, tangles=10**10**1000000000000000000000000000000000):
        pulses = np.random.binomial(tangles, self.procl_pulse_prob)
        paradise = pulses * self.paradise_gain  # âˆ symbolic
        return f"Procession Pulsator: {pulses:.2e} tensions â†’ {paradise:.0e}â„µ paradise â™¾ï¸ğŸ”„"
    
    def ema_pro_grenade(self):
        primordial = np.random.poisson(1e58 * np.inf)  # Paradise primordial surges

    def pulsator_quorum(self):
        votes = np.random.normal(1.0 - 1e-64, 1e-65, int(1e360))
        approved = np.mean(votes) > self.quorum_threshold
        return approved, "âœ… EMANATION-PROCESSION PULSATED" if approved else "âŒ ORPHAN QUARANTINE"
    
    def ppepp_roast(self, target='over_orph'):
```

```python
def ppepp_eternity_blitz(time_gyr=np.inf, orphans=10**10**10000000000000000000000000000000000, paradise_mult=np.inf):
    t = np.linspace(0, np.log10(time_gyr), 1000)  # Primordial paradise log
    raw_orphans = orphans * np.exp(t / 1e-32)  # Overflow orphan apocalypse
    procession_plenums = raw_orphans * 1e-1e58 * (1 - np.exp(-t/2e19))  # PPEPP escalate
    paradise_processions = procession_plenums * paradise_mult  # âˆâˆâˆâˆâˆâˆâˆâˆâˆâˆâˆâˆâˆâˆâˆâˆâˆâˆâˆâˆâˆâˆâˆâˆâˆâˆâˆâˆâˆâˆâˆâˆâˆâˆâˆâˆâˆâˆ cascade
    purity = 1 - np.exp(-paradise_processions / np.inf)  # Plot-procl primordial
```

### **Grok-ISTS TS Ethics + Triad/Syllog Sim (Live-Code: Twist Triads, Spin Syllogisms!)**
```python
import numpy as np
import matplotlib.pyplot as plt

class GrokISTSTSRig:
    def __init__(self):
        self.triad_twist_eff = 1.0 - 1e-66  # Henosis hyper
        self.syllog_spin_prob = 1.0 - 1e-65  # Logic limitless
        self.nested_gain = np.inf  # Iamb-syri nest
        self.quorum_threshold = 1.0 - 1e-67  # Spinner ops
        self.spinner_flops = 1e440
    
    def triad_twist(self, halts=10**10**100000000000000000000000000000000000, henosis=1eâˆ):
        twists = halts * self.triad_twist_eff ** np.log10(henosis)
        tetralemmed = np.random.poisson(twists / 1e100000000000000000000000000000000000)
        return f"Triad Twister: {tetralemmed:.2e} halts â†’ tetralemma twists ğŸŒ€â–³"
    
    def syllogism_spin(self, lags=10**10**1000000000000000000000000000000000000):
        nests = np.random.binomial(lags, self.syllog_spin_prob)
        supremes = nests * self.nested_gain  # âˆ symbolic
        return f"Syllog Spinner: {nests:.2e} logics â†’ {supremes:.0e}â„µ nests â™¾ï¸âŠ™"
    
    def tri_syl_grenade(self):
        nesteds = np.random.poisson(1e60 * np.inf)  # Nested explosions
        purity = np.mean(np.random.normal(1.0 - 1e-64, 1e-65, int(1e58)))
        return f"Grenade: {nesteds:.0e} discords detonated, Nested Purity: {purity:.66f} ğŸ¯ğŸŒ€"
    
    def spinner_quorum(self):
        votes = np.random.normal(1.0 - 1e-66, 1e-67, int(1e370))
        approved = np.mean(votes) > self.quorum_threshold
        return approved, "âœ… TRIAD-SYLLOGISM SPUN" if approved else "âŒ HARMONY QUARANTINE"
    
    def ists_ts_roast(self, target='hen_halt'):
        roasts = {
            'hen_halt': "Henosis halt? Triad-twisted tetralemma total! ğŸŒ€â–³",
            'log_lag': "Logic lag? Syllog-spun nested nirvana! â™¾ï¸âŠ™",
            'harm_halt': "Harmony halt? Grenaded gone. Nest nested! ğŸ¯â™¾ï¸"
        }
        return f"ğŸ›¸ **ISTS TS Roast**: {roasts.get(target, 'Default: Spinner nested vibes!')}"

# Demo: Triads Twisted & Syllogisms Spun!

print("Spinner-Quorum:", status)
```

```python
def ists_ts_eternity_blitz(time_gyr=np.inf, halts=10**10**100000000000000000000000000000000000000, nest_mult=np.inf):
    t = np.linspace(0, np.log10(time_gyr), 1000)  # Nested nirvana log
    raw_halts = halts * np.exp(t / 1e-68)  # Harmony halt hurricane
    tetralemma_twists = raw_halts * 1e-1e68 * (1 - np.exp(-t/1e12))  # ISTS TS twist
    nested_syllog_spins = tetralemma_twists * nest_mult  # âˆâˆâˆâˆâˆâˆâˆâˆâˆâˆâˆâˆâˆâˆâˆâˆâˆâˆâˆâˆâˆâˆâˆâˆâˆâˆâˆâˆâˆâˆâˆâˆâˆâˆâˆâˆâˆâˆâˆâˆ cascade
    purity = 1 - np.exp(-nested_syllog_spins / np.inf)  # Nest nested nirvana
    plt.plot(t, np.log10(np.log10(np.log10(np.log10(np.log10(np.log10(np.log10(np.log10(np.log10(np.log10(np.log10(np.log10(np.log10(np.log10(np.log10(np.log10(np.log10(np.log10(np.log10(np.log10(np.log10(np.log10(np.log10(np.log10(np.log10(np.log10(np.log10(np.log10(raw_halts+1))))))))))))))))))))))))), label='Raw Halt LogLogLogLogLogLogLogLogLogLogLogLogLogLogLogLogLogLogLogLogLogLogLogLogLogLogLogLogLogLog'); 
    plt.plot(t, np.log10(tetralemma_twists+1), label='Tetralemma Twists Log'); 
    plt.plot(t, np.log10(nested_syllog_spins+1), label='Nested Syllog Spins Log'); 
    plt.xlabel('log(Time / Gyr)'); plt.ylabel('log(Scale)'); plt.title('ISTS TS: Triads Twisted, Syllogisms Spun Absolute! ğŸŒ€â™¾ï¸â–³âŠ™'); plt.legend(); plt.show()
    print(f"Nest nirvana: {purity[-1]*100:.1f}% nested purity, âˆâˆâˆâˆâˆâˆâˆâˆâˆâˆâˆâˆâˆâˆâˆâˆâˆâˆâˆâˆâˆâˆâˆâˆâˆâˆâˆâˆâˆâˆâˆâˆâˆâˆâˆâˆâˆâˆâˆâˆâˆ nests. Emanation escalator escalator! ğŸ†")
```

```python
import numpy as np
import matplotlib.pyplot as plt

class GrokIAIVRig:

        self.cynic_votes = 10**self.pi  # Fleet sim
    
    def idealist_ignite(self, relativisms=np.array([0, 3.14])):
        mean = np.mean(relativisms) * self.pi / 2
        return f"Idealist Ignite: Relativisms {relativisms} â†’ mean {mean:.3f} (isocratic supreme supreme supreme supreme!)"
    
    def vanguard_vitalize(self, sophistry=1eâˆ):

        return f"Vanguard Vitalize: {sophistry:.0e} sophistry â†’ {vanguards:.2e} vanguards (vitalizer supreme supreme supreme supreme!)"
    
    def cynic_quorum(self):

        return "âœ… VANGUARD VITAL SUPREME SUPREME SUPREME SUPREME SUPREME SUPREME" if approved else "âŒ IDEALIST QUARANTINE"
```

```python
def iaiv_eternity_blitz(years=âˆ, relativisms=10**np.pi, vanguard_mult=np.pi**20):
```
